<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="English">English</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=child&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: English">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="mw-default-size mw-halign-right" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:MDRBobMomSmall.jpg" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d7/MDRBobMomSmall.jpg/220px-MDRBobMomSmall.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="282" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/d/d7/MDRBobMomSmall.jpg 1.5x" data-file-width="320" data-file-height="410"></a><figcaption>A woman with two children <a href="/wiki/circa" title="circa">c.</a> 1933.</figcaption></figure>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=child&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Etymology 1">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Middle_English">child</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/cild#Old_English" title="cild">ċild</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-West_Germanic/kil%C3%BE&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-West Germanic/kilþ (page does not exist)">*kilþ</a></i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-West_Germanic/kel%C3%BE&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-West Germanic/kelþ (page does not exist)">*kelþ</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/kel%C3%BEaz" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/kelþaz">*kelþaz</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href="/wiki/womb" title="womb">womb</a>; <a href="/wiki/fetus" title="fetus">fetus</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/%C7%B5elt-&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/ǵelt- (page does not exist)">*ǵelt-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href="/wiki/womb" title="womb">womb</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da"><a href="/wiki/kuld#Danish" title="kuld">kuld</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href="/wiki/brood" title="brood">brood</a>, <a href="/wiki/litter" title="litter">litter</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv"><a href="/wiki/kull#Swedish" title="kull">kull</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href="/wiki/brood" title="brood">brood</a>, <a href="/wiki/litter" title="litter">litter</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is"><a href="/wiki/kelta#Icelandic" title="kelta">kelta</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="is"><a href="/wiki/kjalta#Icelandic" title="kjalta">kjalta</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href="/wiki/lap" title="lap">lap</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got"><a href="/wiki/%F0%90%8C%BA%F0%90%8C%B9%F0%90%8C%BB%F0%90%8C%B8%F0%90%8C%B4%F0%90%8C%B9#Gothic" title="𐌺𐌹𐌻𐌸𐌴𐌹">𐌺𐌹𐌻𐌸𐌴𐌹</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn"><a href="/wiki/kil%C3%BEei#Gothic" title="kilþei">kilþei</a></span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href="/wiki/womb" title="womb">womb</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa"><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E0%A4%9C%E0%A4%B0%E0%A5%8D%E0%A4%A4&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="जर्त (page does not exist)">जर्त</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jarta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa"><a href="/wiki/%E0%A4%9C%E0%A4%B0%E0%A5%8D%E0%A4%A4%E0%A5%81#Sanskrit" title="जर्तु">जर्तु</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=child&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">child</strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/children#English" title="children">children</a></b> <i>or</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">dialectal or archaic</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/childer#English" title="childer">childer</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li class="mw-empty-elt"></li><li class="senseid" id="English:_kid_aged_0_to_18_years"> <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#broadly" title="Appendix:Glossary">broadly</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href="/wiki/person" title="person">person</a> who has not yet reached <a href="/wiki/adulthood" title="adulthood">adulthood</a>, whether <a href="/wiki/natural" title="natural">natural</a> (<a href="/wiki/puberty" title="puberty">puberty</a>), <a href="/wiki/cultural" title="cultural">cultural</a> (<a href="/wiki/initiation" title="initiation">initiation</a>), or <a href="/wiki/legal" title="legal">legal</a> (<a href="/wiki/majority" title="majority">majority</a>).
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Go easy on him: he is but a <b>child</b>.</i></div></dd></dl>

<dl><dd>And not just the <b>children</b>, teenagers too. Chuck wants a football, Kathleen a tattoo.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2013</b> June 7,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Joseph_Stiglitz" class="extiw" title="w:Joseph Stiglitz">Joseph Stiglitz</a>,  “Globalisation is about taxes too”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Guardian_Weekly" class="extiw" title="w:The Guardian Weekly">The Guardian Weekly</a></cite>‎<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/commentisfree/2013/may/27/globalisation-is-about-taxes-too">[1]</a></sup>, volume 188, number 26, page 19:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">It is time the international community faced the reality: we have an unmanageable, unfair, distortionary global tax regime. <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> It is the starving of the public sector which has been pivotal in America no longer being the land of opportunity – with a <b>child'</b>s life prospects more dependent on the income and education of its parents than in other advanced countries.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul>

<ol><li class="mw-empty-elt"></li><li class="senseid" id="English:_kid_aged_1_to_11_years"> <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/pediatrics" title="pediatrics">pediatrics</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> sometimes, in a <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#strict" title="Appendix:Glossary">stricter</a> sense</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A kid aged 1 to 11 years, whereas <a href="/wiki/neonate#Noun" title="neonate">neonates</a> are aged 0 to 1 month, <a href="/wiki/infant#Noun" title="infant">infants</a> are aged 1 month to 12 months, and <a href="/wiki/adolescent#Noun" title="adolescent">adolescents</a> are aged 12 years to 18 years.

<li class="mw-empty-elt"></li><li class="senseid" id="English:_figuratively,_of_times_or_tribes"> <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#figurative" title="Appendix:Glossary">figurative</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href="/wiki/figurative" title="figurative">figurative</a> <a href="/wiki/offspring" title="offspring">offspring</a>, <i>particularly:</i>
<ol><li>A person considered a <a href="/wiki/product" title="product">product</a> of a <a href="/wiki/place" title="place">place</a> or <a href="/wiki/culture" title="culture">culture</a>, a <a href="/wiki/member" title="member">member</a> of a <a href="/wiki/tribe" title="tribe">tribe</a> or culture, regardless of age.

<li class="mw-empty-elt"></li><li class="senseid" id="English:_female_child,_obsoletely"> <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#obsolete" title="Appendix:Glossary">obsolete</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> specifically</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href="/wiki/female" title="female">female</a> child, a <a href="/wiki/girl" title="girl">girl</a>.

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=child&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Etymology 2">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/childen#Middle_English" title="childen">childen</a></i>, from the noun <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Middle_English">child</a></i>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=child&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Verb">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">child</strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3|s|pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/childs#English" title="childs">childs</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres|ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/childing#English" title="childing">childing</a></b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past|and|past|ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/childed#English" title="childed">childed</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#archaic" title="Appendix:Glossary">archaic</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/transitive" title="transitive">transitive</a>, <a href="/wiki/intransitive" title="intransitive">intransitive</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To <a href="/wiki/give_birth" title="give birth">give birth</a>; to <a href="/wiki/beget" title="beget">beget</a> or <a href="/wiki/procreate" title="procreate">procreate</a>.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1596</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edmund_Spenser" class="extiw" title="w:Edmund Spenser">Edmund Spenser</a>,  “Book VI, Canto XII”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Faerie_Queene" class="extiw" title="w:The Faerie Queene">The Faerie Queene.<span class="q-hellip-sp">&nbsp;</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="Disposed into Twelue Bookes, Fashioning XII. Morall Vertues.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></a></cite>, part II (books IV–VI), London: <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="Imprinted at London [by]">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> [<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Richard_Field_(printer)" class="extiw" title="w:Richard Field (printer)">Richard Field</a>] for <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Ponsonby_(publisher)" class="extiw" title="w:William Ponsonby (publisher)">William Ponsonby</a>, <small><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://worldcat.org/oclc/932900760">→OCLC</a></small>, stanza 17, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://archive.org/details/faeriequeenedisp02spen/page/512/mode/1up">page 512</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">My liefe (ſayd ſhe) ye know, that long ygo, <br> Whileſt ye in durance dwelt, ye to me gaue <br> A little mayde, the which ye <b>chylded</b> tho&nbsp;; <br> The ſame againe if now ye liſt to haue, <br> The ſame is yonder Lady, whom high God did ſaue.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1600</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Torquato_Tasso" class="extiw" title="w:Torquato Tasso">[Torquato Tasso]</a>,  “The Eighteenth Booke of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Godfrey_of_Bouillon" class="extiw" title="w:Godfrey of Bouillon"><i>Godfrey</i> of Bulloigne</a>”, in Edward Fairefax [<i>i.e.</i>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edward_Fairfax" class="extiw" title="w:Edward Fairfax">Edward Fairfax</a>], transl., <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jerusalem_Delivered" class="extiw" title="w:Jerusalem Delivered">Godfrey of Bulloigne, or The Recouerie of Ierusalem.<span class="q-hellip-sp">&nbsp;</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="Done into English Heroicall Verse, by Edward Fairefax Gent.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></a></cite>, London: <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="Imprinted at London by">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> Ar[nold] Hatfield, for I[saac] Iaggard and M[atthew] Lownes, <small><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://worldcat.org/oclc/940138160">→OCLC</a></small>, stanza 26, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://archive.org/details/godfreyofbulloig00tass_0/page/320/mode/1up">page 320</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">And from his fertill hollow wombe forth ran, <br> (Clad in rare weedes and ſtrange habiliment) <br> A Nymph, for age able to goe to man, <br> An hundreth plants beſide (euen in his ſight) <br> <b>Childed</b> an hundreth Nymphes, ſo great, ſo dight:<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#c." title="Appendix:Glossary"><abbr title="circa">c.</abbr></a></i> <b>1603–1606</b> (date written),  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">[William Shakespeare]</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/King_Lear" class="extiw" title="w:King Lear"><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="M. By His Maiesties Seruants Playing vsually at the Gloabe on the Bancke-side.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></a></cite> (First Quarto), London: <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="Printed for">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nathaniel_Butter" class="extiw" title="w:Nathaniel Butter">Nathaniel Butter</a>,<span class="q-hellip-sp">&nbsp;</span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="and are to be sold at his shop in Pauls Church-yard at the signe of the Pide Bull neere St. Austins Gate.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, published 1608, <small><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://worldcat.org/oclc/54196469">→OCLC</a></small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.co.nz/books?id=7l4zAQAAMAAJ&amp;pg=PP64">[Act III, scene v]</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><span class="q-hellip-sp"></span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span>But then the mind much ſufferance doth or'e ſcip, <br> When griefe hath mates,​and bearing fellowſhip&nbsp;: <br> How light and portable my paine ſeemes now, <br> When that which makes me bend, makes the King bow, <br> He <b>childed</b> as I fathered,​<i>Tom</i> away, <br> Marke the high noyſes and thy ſelfe bewray,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Middle_English">Middle English</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=child&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Middle English">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Alternative_forms_2">Alternative forms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=child&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Alternative forms">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/chyld#Middle_English" title="chyld">chyld</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/chylde#Middle_English" title="chylde">chylde</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/childe#Middle_English" title="childe">childe</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/chelde#Middle_English" title="chelde">chelde</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/cild#Middle_English" title="cild">cild</a></span></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=child&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/cild#Old_English" title="cild">ċild</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/kel%C3%BEaz" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/kelþaz">*kelþaz</a></i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_2">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=child&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Middle_English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:Middle English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/tʃiːld/</span></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=child&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="enm">child</strong> (<i>plural</i> <b><span class="Latn" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/children#Middle_English" title="children">children</a></span></b> <i>or</i> <b><span class="Latn" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/childre#Middle_English" title="childre">childre</a></span></b> <i>or</i> <b><span class="Latn" lang="enm"><strong class="selflink">child</strong></span></b> <i>or</i> <b><span class="Latn" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/childres#Middle_English" title="childres">childres</a></span></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <a href="/wiki/baby" title="baby">baby</a>, <a href="/wiki/infant" title="infant">infant</a>, <a href="/wiki/toddler" title="toddler">toddler</a>; a person in <a href="/wiki/infancy" title="infancy">infancy</a>.</li>
<li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#English">child</a></span>, <a href="/wiki/kid" title="kid">kid</a>; a young person.</li>
<li>An <a href="/wiki/offspring" title="offspring">offspring</a>, one of one's <a href="/wiki/progeny" title="progeny">progeny</a>.</li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/childish" title="childish">childish</a> or <a href="/wiki/stupid" title="stupid">stupid</a> <a href="/wiki/individual" title="individual">individual</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Chrisitanity</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The <a href="/wiki/Christ_child" title="Christ child">Christ child</a>; <a href="/wiki/Jesus" title="Jesus">Jesus</a> as a <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#English">child</a></span>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#figurative" title="Appendix:Glossary">figurative</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A member of a creed <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">usually with the religion in the genitive preposing it</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>A young male, especially one employed as an <a href="/wiki/hireling" title="hireling">hireling</a>.</li>
<li>A young noble training to become a knight; a <a href="/wiki/squire" title="squire">squire</a> or <a href="/wiki/childe" title="childe">childe</a>.</li>
<li>The young of <a href="/wiki/animals" title="animals">animals</a> or <a href="/wiki/plants" title="plants">plants</a>.</li>
<li>A material as a <a href="/wiki/result" title="result">result</a> or <a href="/wiki/outcome" title="outcome">outcome</a>.</li></ol>
